# __tests__\process-pdf.test.ts

```ts
/// <reference types="jest" /> import { describe, it, expect, jest, beforeEach } from '@jest/globals'; import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import { POST } from '../app/api/process-pdf/route'; import { PDFProcessor } from '../utils/pdf-processor'; // Types for mocks interface MockPDFProcessor { downloadPDF: jest.Mock<Promise<Buffer>, [string]>; extractTextFromPDF: jest.Mock<Promise<string>, [Buffer]>; } // Mock NextResponse jest.mock('next/server', () => ({ NextRequest: function(input: string | URL, init?: RequestInit) { return Object.assign(new Request(input, init), { nextUrl: new URL(typeof input === 'string' ? input : input.toString()), cookies: new Map(), page: { name: 'test' }, ua: { isBot: false } }); }, NextResponse: { json: (data: any) => ({ status: 200, headers: new Headers({ 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }), json: async () => data }) } })); // Mock PDFProcessor with typed mock functions jest.mock('../utils/pdf-processor', () => ({ PDFProcessor: { downloadPDF: jest.fn<Promise<Buffer>, [string]>(), extractTextFromPDF: jest.fn<Promise<string>, [Buffer]>() } })); describe('PDF Processing API Route', () => { let mockPDFProcessor: MockPDFProcessor; beforeEach(() => { jest.clearAllMocks(); mockPDFProcessor = PDFProcessor as unknown as MockPDFProcessor; }); it('should successfully process a PDF file', async () => { // Mock data const mockPdfBuffer = Buffer.from('mock pdf content'); const mockExtractedText = 'Sample PDF content'; const mockFilePath = 'test/sample.pdf'; // Mock PDFProcessor methods with proper types mockPDFProcessor.downloadPDF.mockResolvedValue(mockPdfBuffer); mockPDFProcessor.extractTextFromPDF.mockResolvedValue(mockExtractedText); // Create mock request using NextRequest const mockRequest = new NextRequest(new URL('http://localhost:3000/api/process-pdf'), { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ filepath: mockFilePath }) }); // Call the API route const response = await POST(mockRequest); const data = await response.json(); // Assertions expect(data).toEqual({ success: true, fileSize: mockPdfBuffer.length, textLength: mockExtractedText.length, textPreview: mockExtractedText.substring(0, 200), filepath: mockFilePath }); // Verify PDFProcessor methods were called expect(mockPDFProcessor.downloadPDF).toHaveBeenCalledWith(mockFilePath); expect(mockPDFProcessor.extractTextFromPDF).toHaveBeenCalledWith(mockPdfBuffer); }); it('should handle PDF processing errors', async () => { // Mock error const mockError = new Error('PDF processing failed'); mockPDFProcessor.downloadPDF.mockRejectedValue(mockError); // Create mock request using NextRequest const mockRequest = new NextRequest(new URL('http://localhost:3000/api/process-pdf'), { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ filepath: 'test/error.pdf' }) }); // Call the API route const response = await POST(mockRequest); const data = await response.json(); // Assertions expect(data).toEqual({ error: 'PDF processing failed', details: mockError.message }); }); });
```

# app\api\chapters\[chapterId]\cards\route.ts

```ts
// app/api/chapters/[chapterId]/cards/route.ts import { createRouteHandlerClient } from '@supabase/auth-helpers-nextjs'; import { cookies } from 'next/headers'; import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'; export async function GET( request: Request, { params }: { params: { chapterId: string } } ) { const supabase = createRouteHandlerClient({ cookies }); try { // Get user session const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser(); if (authError || !user) { return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 }); } // Get learning items for this chapter const { data: learningItems, error: itemsError } = await supabase .from('learning_items') .select(` id, type, content, metadata, difficulty, user_progress ( times_shown, times_correct, times_incorrect, next_review_at ) `) .eq('chapter_id', params.chapterId) .eq('user_progress.user_id', user.id) .order('next_review_at', { nullsFirst: true }); if (itemsError) throw itemsError; // Filter items due for review const now = new Date(); const dueItems = learningItems.filter(item => { const progress = item.user_progress[0]; return !progress || !progress.next_review_at || new Date(progress.next_review_at) <= now; }); return NextResponse.json({ cards: dueItems.map(item => ({ id: item.id, type: item.type, ...(item.type === 'flashcard' ? { content: { front: item.content.front, back: item.content.back } } : { content: { question: item.content.question, options: item.content.options } } ), difficulty: item.difficulty, progress: item.user_progress[0] || null })) }); } catch (error) { console.error('Error fetching cards:', error); return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to fetch cards' }, { status: 500 }); } }
```

# app\api\learning-progress\route.ts

```ts
// app/api/learning-progress/route.ts import { createRouteHandlerClient } from '@supabase/auth-helpers-nextjs'; import { cookies } from 'next/headers'; import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'; function calculateNextReview(progress: any, isCorrect: boolean) { const easeFactor = progress?.ease_factor || 2.5; const currentInterval = progress?.interval_days || 1; if (isCorrect) { // Increase interval using SuperMemo-2 algorithm const newInterval = currentInterval * easeFactor; const newEaseFactor = easeFactor + (0.1 - (5 - 5) * (0.08 + (5 - 5) * 0.02)); return { interval_days: Math.round(newInterval), ease_factor: Math.max(1.3, newEaseFactor), next_review_at: new Date(Date.now() + newInterval * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) }; } else { // Reset interval for incorrect answers return { interval_days: 1, ease_factor: Math.max(1.3, easeFactor - 0.2), next_review_at: new Date(Date.now() + 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) }; } } export async function POST(request: Request) { const supabase = createRouteHandlerClient({ cookies }); try { const { cardId, isCorrect } = await request.json(); // Get user session const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser(); if (authError || !user) { return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 }); } // Get current progress const { data: progress, error: progressError } = await supabase .from('user_progress') .select('*') .eq('user_id', user.id) .eq('learning_item_id', cardId) .single(); if (progressError && progressError.code !== 'PGRST116') { // Not found error throw progressError; } // Calculate next review time const nextReview = calculateNextReview(progress, isCorrect); // Update or insert progress const { error: upsertError } = await supabase .from('user_progress') .upsert({ user_id: user.id, // Agora é seguro usar user.id pois verificamos acima learning_item_id: cardId, times_shown: (progress?.times_shown || 0) + 1, times_correct: (progress?.times_correct || 0) + (isCorrect ? 1 : 0), times_incorrect: (progress?.times_incorrect || 0) + (isCorrect ? 0 : 1), last_shown_at: new Date(), ...nextReview }); if (upsertError) throw upsertError; return NextResponse.json({ success: true }); } catch (error) { console.error('Error updating progress:', error); return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to update progress' }, { status: 500 }); } }
```

# app\api\private.ts

```ts
import { GetServerSideProps } from 'next'; import { createServerClient } from '@/utils/supabase/server'; export const getServerSideProps: GetServerSideProps = async ({ req, res }) => { const supabase = createServerClient(req, res); const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.getUser(); if (error || !data.user) { return { redirect: { destination: '/login', permanent: false, }, }; } return { props: { user: data.user } }; }; export default function PrivatePage({ user }) { return <p>Welcome, {user.email}</p>; }
```

# app\api\process-pdf\route.ts

```ts
// app/api/pdf/route.ts import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'; import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'; import * as pdfjsLib from 'pdfjs-dist/legacy/build/pdf.js'; // Set up the worker source (required for PDF.js) pdfjsLib.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/pdf.js/3.11.174/pdf.worker.js'; export async function POST(req: NextRequest) { try { const { filepath } = await req.json(); // Get Supabase client const supabase = createClient( process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!, process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY! ); // Get file URL const { data: urlData } = await supabase .storage .from('pdf-bucket') .createSignedUrl(filepath, 3600); if (!urlData?.signedUrl) { throw new Error('Could not get signed URL'); } // Load the PDF directly from URL const pdf = await pdfjsLib.getDocument(urlData.signedUrl).promise; // Get number of pages const numPages = pdf.numPages; // Extract text from each page let fullText = ''; for (let i = 1; i <= numPages; i++) { const page = await pdf.getPage(i); const content = await page.getTextContent(); const pageText = content.items .map((item: any) => item.str) .join(' '); fullText += pageText + '\n'; } return NextResponse.json({ success: true, text: fullText, pages: numPages }); } catch (error) { console.error('PDF Processing error:', error); return NextResponse.json( { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to process PDF' }, { status: 500 } ); } }
```

# app\chapters\page.tsx

```tsx
// app/chapters/page.tsx 'use client'; import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'; import Link from 'next/link'; import { createClient } from '@/utils/supabase/client'; interface Chapter { id: string; title: string; sequence_number: number; status: 'locked' | 'unlocked' | 'completed'; progress?: { completed: number; total: number; mastery: number; }; } export default function ChaptersPage() { const [chapters, setChapters] = useState<Chapter[]>([]); const supabase = createClient(); useEffect(() => { async function loadChapters() { const { data, error } = await supabase .from('chapters') .select(` id, title, sequence_number, status `) .order('sequence_number'); if (error) { console.error('Error loading chapters:', error); return; } setChapters(data || []); } loadChapters(); }, []); return ( <div className="container mx-auto p-4"> <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">Capítulos</h1> <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3"> {chapters.map((chapter) => ( <Link key={chapter.id} href={`/learn/${chapter.id}`} className={`p-4 rounded-lg border ${ chapter.status === 'locked' ? 'bg-gray-100 cursor-not-allowed' : 'hover:shadow-lg transition-shadow' }`} > <div className="flex justify-between items-start"> <div> <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Capítulo {chapter.sequence_number}</h2> <p className="text-gray-600">{chapter.title}</p> </div> {chapter.progress && ( <div className="text-right"> <p className="text-sm text-gray-500"> {chapter.progress.completed}/{chapter.progress.total} </p> <p className="text-sm text-blue-600"> {chapter.progress.mastery.toFixed(1)}% mastery </p> </div> )} </div> </Link> ))} </div> </div> ); }
```

# app\learn\[chapterId]\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'; import { CardViewer } from '@/components/learning/CardViewer'; import { ProgressBar } from '@/components/learning/ProgressBar'; import { LearningService } from '@/lib/learning-service'; import type { FlashCard, QuizCard } from '@/types/learning'; export default function ChapterLearningPage({ params }: { params: { chapterId: string } }) { const [cards, setCards] = useState<Array<FlashCard | QuizCard>>([]); const [progress, setProgress] = useState({ completed: 0, total: 0, mastery: 0 }); useEffect(() => { const loadChapter = async () => { try { const response = await fetch(`/api/chapters/${params.chapterId}/cards`); const data = await response.json(); setCards(data.cards); const chapterProgress = await LearningService.getChapterProgress(params.chapterId); setProgress({ completed: chapterProgress.masteredItems, total: chapterProgress.totalItems, mastery: chapterProgress.percentComplete }); } catch (error) { console.error('Error loading chapter:', error); } }; loadChapter(); }, [params.chapterId]); const handleCardComplete = async (cardId: string, isCorrect: boolean) => { try { await fetch('/api/learning-progress', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ cardId, isCorrect }) }); await LearningService.unlockNextChapter(params.chapterId); const newProgress = await LearningService.getChapterProgress(params.chapterId); setProgress({ completed: newProgress.masteredItems, total: newProgress.totalItems, mastery: newProgress.percentComplete }); } catch (error) { console.error('Error updating progress:', error); } }; return ( <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100"> <ProgressBar current={progress.completed} total={progress.total} mastery={progress.mastery} /> <CardViewer cards={cards} onCardComplete={handleCardComplete} /> </div> ); }
```

# app\login\actions.ts

```ts
"use client"; import { createClient } from '../../utils/supabase/client'; import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'; export async function handleGoogleLogin() { const supabase = createClient(); const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOAuth({ provider: 'google', options: { redirectTo: `${location.origin}/auth/callback`, }, }); if (error) { console.error('Error:', error.message); return; } } export async function handleLogout() { const router = useRouter(); const supabase = createClient(); const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut(); if (error) { console.error('Error:', error.message); return; } router.refresh(); router.push('/'); }
```

```tsx
'use client'; import { TestProcessor } from '@/components/TestProcessor'; import PDFUploader from '@/components/pdf/PDFUploader'; import Link from 'next/link'; import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'; import { createClient } from '@/utils/supabase/client'; import { TestPdfProcessor } from '@/components/TestPDFProcessor'; import { PDFProcessorComponent } from '@/components/PDFProcessor'; interface Stats { documentsCount: number; chaptersCount: number; flashcardsCount: number; quizzesCount: number; } export default function Home() { const [stats, setStats] = useState<Stats>({ documentsCount: 0, chaptersCount: 0, flashcardsCount: 0, quizzesCount: 0 }); useEffect(() => { async function loadStats() { const supabase = createClient(); try { // Get documents count const { count: docsCount } = await supabase .from('pdfs') .select('*', { count: 'exact' }); // Get chapters count const { count: chaptersCount } = await supabase .from('chapters') .select('*', { count: 'exact' }); flashcardsCount, quizzesCount }); } catch (error) { console.error('Error loading stats:', error); } } loadStats(); }, []); return ( <main className="flex min-h-screen flex-col items-center justify-between p-24"> <div className="z-10 max-w-5xl w-full items-center justify-between font-mono text-sm"> <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-8">PDF Learning App</h1> {/* Navigation & Summary */} font-bold">{stats.flashcardsCount}</p> </div> <div className="p-4 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg"> <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Quizzes</p> <p className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats.quizzesCount}</p> <Link href="/progress" className="flex-1 p-4 bg-gray-100 rounded-lg text-center hover:bg-gray-200 transition-colors" > View Progress </Link> </div> </div> {/* PDF Upload Section */} <div # app\study\page.tsx
```

```tsx
'use client'; import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'; import { createClientComponentClient } from '@supabase/auth-helpers-nextjs'; import { FlashCard } from '@/components/cards/FlashCard'; import { QuizCard } from '@/components/cards/QuizCard'; import { Card } from '@/components/ui/card'; import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'; import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'; type StudyCard = { id: string; type: 'flashcard' | 'quiz'; content: { front?: string; back?: string; question?: string; options?: Array<{ id: string; text: string; is_correct: boolean; feedback: string; }>; explanation?: string; }; metadata: { difficulty: 'basic' | 'intermediate' | 'advanced'; conceptType: string; prerequisites: string[]; learningObjective: string; }; }; export default function StudyPage() { const [cards, setCards] = useState<StudyCard[]>([]); const [currentIndex, setCurrentIndex] = useState(0); const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true); const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null); const supabase = createClientComponentClient(); const router = useRouter(); useEffect(() => { async function loadCards() { try { const { data: { session } } = await supabase.auth.getSession(); if (!session) { router.push('/login'); return; } const { data: cardsData, error: cardsError } = await supabase .from('cards') .select('*') .eq('user_id', session.user.id) .order('created_at', { ascending: false }); if (cardsError) { throw cardsError; } if (cardsData) { setCards(cardsData as StudyCard[]); } } catch (err) { setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to load study cards'); } finally { setLoading(false); } } loadCards(); }, [supabase, router]); const handleNext = () => { if (currentIndex < cards.length - 1) { setCurrentIndex(prev => prev + 1); } }; const handlePrevious = () => { if (currentIndex > 0) { setCurrentIndex(prev => prev - 1); } }; if (loading) { return ( <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen"> <div className="text-lg">Loading your study materials...</div> </div> ); } if (error) { return ( <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-4"> <Card className="p-6 max-w-md w-full"> <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-red-600 mb-4">Error</h2> <p className="mb-4">{error}</p> <Button onClick={() => window.location.reload()}> Try Again </Button> </Card> </div> ); } if (cards.length === 0) { return ( <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-4"> <Card className="p-6 max-w-md w-full"> <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">No Study Materials</h2> <p className="mb-4">You haven&apos;t created any study materials yet.</p> <Button onClick={() => router.push('/chapters')}> Go to Chapters </Button> </Card> </div> ); } const currentCard = cards[currentIndex]; const isFlashCard = currentCard.type === 'flashcard'; return ( <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-4"> <div className="w-full max-w-2xl"> {isFlashCard ? ( <FlashCard front={currentCard.content.front || ''} back={currentCard.content.back || ''} onSwipeRight={handleNext} onSwipeLeft={handlePrevious} /> ) : ( <QuizCard question={currentCard.content.question || ''} options={currentCard.content.options || []} explanation={currentCard.content.explanation || ''} onAnswer={() => handleNext()} /> )} <div className="flex justify-between mt-4"> <Button onClick={handlePrevious} disabled={currentIndex === 0} variant="outline" > Previous </Button> <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground"> {currentIndex + 1} of {cards.length} </div> <Button onClick={handleNext} disabled={currentIndex === cards.length - 1} > Next </Button> </div> </div> </div> ); }
```

```ts
// types/learning.ts export interface FlashCard { id: string; type: 'flashcard'; content: { front: string; back: string; }; metadata?: { difficulty: 'basic' | 'intermediate' | 'advanced'; conceptType: string; prerequisites: string[]; learningObjective: string; }; } export interface QuizOption { id: string; text: string; isCorrect: boolean; feedback: string; } export interface QuizCard { id: string; type: 'quiz'; content: { question: string; options: QuizOption[]; explanation: string; }; metadata?: { difficulty: 'basic' | 'intermediate' | 'advanced'; conceptType: string; prerequisites: string[]; learningObjective: string; }; } export interface UserProgress { id: string; userId: string; learningItemId: string; timesShown: number; timesCorrect: number; timesIncorrect: number; lastShownAt: Date; nextReviewAt: Date; easeFactor: number; intervalDays: number; } export type LearningItem = FlashCard | QuizCard;
```

```tsx
'use client'; import React from 'react'; import { Button } from './ui/button'; export function APITester() { const testGET = async () => { try { const response = await fetch('/api/test'); const data = await response.json(); console.log('GET Test response:', data); } catch (error) { console.error('GET Test error:', error); } }; const testPOST = async () => { try { const response = await fetch('/api/test', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', }, body: JSON.stringify({ test: 'data' }), }); const data = await response.json(); console.log('POST Test response:', data); } catch (error) { console.error('POST Test error:', error); } }; return ( <div className="space-x-4"> <Button onClick={testGET}>Test GET</Button> <Button onClick={testPOST}>Test POST</Button> </div> ); }
```

# components\cards\FlashCard.tsx

```tsx
// components/cards/FlashCard.tsx 'use client'; import { useState } from 'react'; import { Card, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card"; interface FlashCardProps { front: string; back: string; onSwipeRight?: () => void; onSwipeLeft?: () => void; } export function FlashCard({ front, back, onSwipeRight, onSwipeLeft }: FlashCardProps) { const [isFlipped, setIsFlipped] = useState(false); const [startX, setStartX] = useState(0); const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false); const [dragOffset, setDragOffset] = useState(0); const handleTouchStart = (e: React.TouchEvent | React.MouseEvent) => { setStartX('touches' in e ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX); setIsDragging(true); }; const handleTouchMove = (e: React.TouchEvent | React.MouseEvent) => { if (!isDragging) return; const currentX = 'touches' in e ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX; const offset = currentX - startX; setDragOffset(offset); }; const handleTouchEnd = () => { if (Math.abs(dragOffset) > 100) { // threshold for swipe if (dragOffset > 0) { onSwipeRight?.(); } else { onSwipeLeft?.(); } } setIsDragging(false); setDragOffset(0); }; return ( <div className="w-full max-w-xl mx-auto perspective-1000" onMouseDown={handleTouchStart} onMouseMove={handleTouchMove} onMouseUp={handleTouchEnd} onTouchStart={handleTouchStart} onTouchMove={handleTouchMove as any} onTouchEnd={handleTouchEnd} > <Card className={`transform-style-3d transition-transform duration-500 cursor-pointer ${ isFlipped ? 'rotate-y-180' : '' }`} style={{ transform: `rotateY(${isFlipped ? '180deg' : '0'}) translateX(${dragOffset}px)`, }} onClick={() => setIsFlipped(!isFlipped)} > <CardContent className="p-6 h-64 flex items-center justify-center backface-hidden"> <p className="text-lg text-center">{isFlipped ? back : front}</p> </CardContent> </Card> </div> ); }
```

# components\cards\QuizCard.tsx

```tsx
// components/cards/QuizCard.tsx 'use client'; import { useState } from 'react'; // Adicionando import do useState import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card"; import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"; import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"; interface Option { id: string; text: string; is_correct: boolean; feedback: string; } interface QuizCardProps { question: string; options: Option[]; explanation: string; onAnswer: (isCorrect: boolean) => void; } export function QuizCard({ question, options, explanation, onAnswer }: QuizCardProps) { const [selectedOption, setSelectedOption] = useState<string | null>(null); const [showFeedback, setShowFeedback] = useState(false); const handleOptionClick = (option: Option) => { setSelectedOption(option.id); setShowFeedback(true); onAnswer(option.is_correct); }; return ( <Card className="w-full max-w-xl mx-auto"> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>{question}</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent className="space-y-4"> {options.map((option) => ( <Button key={option.id} variant={selectedOption === option.id ? (option.is_correct ? "default" : "destructive") // Mudando "success" para "default" : "outline" } className={cn( "w-full justify-start text-left", selectedOption === option.id && option.is_correct && "bg-green-500 hover:bg-green-600" )} onClick={() => handleOptionClick(option)} disabled={showFeedback} > {option.text} </Button> ))} {showFeedback && ( <div className="mt-4 p-4 bg-muted rounded-lg"> <p className="font-medium mb-2"> {options.find(opt => opt.id === selectedOption)?.feedback} </p> <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{explanation}</p> </div> )} </CardContent> </Card> ); }
```

# components\learning\CardViewer.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useState, useCallback } from 'react'; import { motion, AnimatePresence, PanInfo } from 'framer-motion'; import { QuizCardContent } from './QuizCardContent'; import { QuizFeedback } from './QuizFeedback'; import type { FlashCard, QuizCard, LearningItem } from '../../app/types/learning'; interface CardViewerProps { cards: LearningItem[]; onCardComplete: (cardId: string, isCorrect: boolean) => void; } export function CardViewer({ cards, onCardComplete }: CardViewerProps) { const [currentIndex, setCurrentIndex] = useState(0); const [isFlipped, setIsFlipped] = useState(false); const [dragStartX, setDragStartX] = useState(0); const [exitX, setExitX] = useState(0); const [selectedOption, setSelectedOption] = useState(''); const handleDragStart = (event: MouseEvent | TouchEvent) => { const clientX = 'touches' in event ? event.touches[0].clientX : event.clientX; setDragStartX(clientX); }; const handleDragEnd = (event: MouseEvent | TouchEvent | PointerEvent, info: PanInfo) => { const clientX = 'changedTouches' in event ? event.changedTouches[0].clientX : event.clientX; const dragDistance = clientX - dragStartX; const threshold = window.innerWidth * 0.4; if (Math.abs(dragDistance) > threshold) { const isCorrect = dragDistance > 0; setExitX(dragDistance); onCardComplete(cards[currentIndex].id, isCorrect); setTimeout(() => { setCurrentIndex(prev => (prev + 1) % cards.length); setIsFlipped(false); setExitX(0); setSelectedOption(''); }, 300); } }; const handleKeyPress = (event: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => { if (event.key === 'ArrowLeft') { setExitX(-window.innerWidth); onCardComplete(cards[currentIndex].id, false); } else if (event.key === 'ArrowRight') { setExitX(window.innerWidth); onCardComplete(cards[currentIndex].id, true); } }; const currentCard = cards[currentIndex]; const handleSelect = (option: any) => { setSelectedOption(option.id); }; return ( <div className="h-screen w-full flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-100" onKeyDown={handleKeyPress} tabIndex={0}> <AnimatePresence> <motion.div key={currentCard.id} className="w-[90vw] h-[70vh] relative perspective-1000" initial={{ x: 0, rotateY: 0 }} animate={{ x: exitX, rotateY: isFlipped ? 180 : 0 }} exit={{ x: exitX }} onDragStart={handleDragStart} onDragEnd={handleDragEnd} drag="x" dragConstraints={{ left: 0, right: 0 }} whileDrag={{ scale: 1.05 }} onClick={() => setIsFlipped(!isFlipped)} > <div className={`w-full h-full rounded-xl shadow-lg bg-white p-6 ${isFlipped ? 'rotate-y-180' : ''} transition-transform duration-500`}> <div className="absolute inset-0 backface-hidden"> {'question' in currentCard ? ( <QuizCardContent card={currentCard as QuizCard} onSelect={handleSelect} /> ) : ( <div className="text-xl font-medium text-center"> {(currentCard as FlashCard).content.front} </div> )} </div> <div className="absolute inset-0 rotate-y-180 backface-hidden"> {'question' in currentCard ? ( <QuizFeedback card={currentCard as QuizCard} selectedOption={selectedOption} /> ) : ( <div className="text-xl text-center"> {(currentCard as FlashCard).content.back} </div> )} </div> </div> </motion.div> </AnimatePresence> </div> ); }
```

```tsx
// components/learning/ProgressBar.tsx interface ProgressBarProps { current: number; total: number; mastery?: number; } export function ProgressBar({ current, total, mastery }: ProgressBarProps) { const progress = (current / total) * 100; return ( <div className="fixed top-0 left-0 w-full"> <div className="h-2 bg-gray-200"> <div className="h-full bg-blue-500 transition-all duration-300" style={{ width: `${progress}%` }} /> </div> {mastery !== undefined && ( <div className="px-4 py-2 text-sm text-gray-600"> Mastery: {mastery.toFixed(1)}% </div> )} </div> ); }
```

```tsx
import { QuizCard, QuizOption } from '../../app/types/learning'; interface QuizFeedbackProps { card: QuizCard; selectedOption?: string; } export function QuizFeedback({ card, selectedOption }: QuizFeedbackProps) { const option = card.content.options.find(opt => opt.id === selectedOption); return ( <div className="space-y-4"> <div className="text-xl font-medium mb-4">{card.content.question}</div> {option && ( <div className={`p-4 rounded-lg ${option.isCorrect ? 'bg-green-50' : 'bg-red-50'}`}> <p className="font-medium">{option.feedback}</p> </div> )} <div className="mt-4"> <p className="text-gray-700">{card.content.explanation}</p> </div> </div> ); }
```

```tsx
import * as React from "react" import Link from "next/link" import { NavItem } from "@/types/nav" import { siteConfig } from "@/config/site" import { cn } from "@/lib/utils" import { Icons } from "@/components/icons" interface MainNavProps { items?: NavItem[] } export function MainNav({ items }: MainNavProps) { return ( <div className="flex gap-6 md:gap-10"> <Link href="/" className="flex items-center space-x-2"> <Icons.logo className="h-6 w-6" /> <span className="inline-block font-bold">{siteConfig.name}</span> </Link> {items?.length ? ( <nav className="flex gap-6"> {items?.map( (item, index) => item.href && ( <Link key={index} href={item.href} className={cn( "flex items-center text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground", item.disabled && "cursor-not-allowed opacity-80" )} > {item.title} </Link> ) )} </nav> ) : null} </div> ) }
```

# components\pdf\PDFUploader.tsx

```tsx
'use client'; import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react'; import { Upload, FileText, X, AlertCircle, Loader2, Check } from 'lucide-react'; import { Alert, AlertDescription } from '@/components/ui/alert'; import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress'; import { Card, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card'; import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'; // Precisamos adicionar este componente import { UploadService } from '@/lib/upload-service'; import { FileWithStatus } from '@/types'; const PDFUploader = () => { const [dragActive, setDragActive] = useState(false); const [error, setError] = useState(''); const [files, setFiles] = useState<FileWithStatus[]>([]); const [selectedFiles, setSelectedFiles] = useState<FileWithStatus[]>([]); useEffect(() => { UploadService.initializeStorage().catch(console.error); }, []); const handleDrag = (e: React.DragEvent) => { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); if (e.type === "dragenter" || e.type === "dragover") { setDragActive(true); } else if (e.type === "dragleave") { setDragActive(false); } }; const handleDrop = async (e: React.DragEvent) => { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); setDragActive(false); const newFiles = Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files); await handleFiles(newFiles); }; const handleChange = async (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => { if (e.target.files) { const newFiles = Array.from(e.target.files); await handleFiles(newFiles); } }; const handleFiles = async (newFiles: File[]) => { const invalidFiles = newFiles.filter(file => file.type !== 'application/pdf'); if (invalidFiles.length > 0) { setError(`${invalidFiles.length} file(s) were not PDFs and were excluded`); return; } const fileObjects: FileWithStatus[] = newFiles.map(file => ({ id: Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9), file, name: file.name, size: file.size, progress: 0, status: 'pending', error: null, filepath: null })); setSelectedFiles(prev => [...prev, ...fileObjects]); }; const handleUpload = async (fileObj: FileWithStatus) => { setFiles(prev => [...prev, { ...fileObj, status: 'uploading' }]); setSelectedFiles(prev => prev.filter(f => f.id !== fileObj.id)); try { const { filepath, error } = await UploadService.uploadPDF( fileObj.file, (progress) => { setFiles(prev => prev.map(f => f.id === fileObj.id ? { ...f, progress } : f )); } ); if (error) throw new Error(error); setFiles(prev => prev.map(f => f.id === fileObj.id ? { ...f, status: 'complete', filepath } : f )); } catch (err) { setFiles(prev => prev.map(f => f.id === fileObj.id ? { ...f, status: 'error', error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Upload failed' } : f )); } }; const handleUploadAll = () => { selectedFiles.forEach(file => handleUpload(file)); }; const handleDelete = async (id: string, isSelected: boolean = false) => { if (isSelected) { setSelectedFiles(prev => prev.filter(f => f.id !== id)); return; } const file = files.find(f => f.id === id); if (file?.filepath) { const { error } = await UploadService.deletePDF(file.filepath); if (error) { setError(`Failed to delete ${file.name}: ${error}`); return; } } setFiles(prev => prev.filter(f => f.id !== id)); }; const formatFileSize = (bytes: number): string => { if (bytes === 0) return '0 Bytes'; const k = 1024; const sizes = ['Bytes', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB']; const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k)); return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(2)) + ' ' + sizes[i]; }; return ( <Card className="w-full max-w-2xl"> <CardContent className="p-6 space-y-4"> {/* Upload Zone */} <div className={`relative border-2 border-dashed rounded-lg p-8 text-center ${dragActive ? 'border-blue-500 bg-blue-50' : 'border-gray-300'} transition-all duration-200 ease-in-out`} onDragEnter={handleDrag} onDragLeave={handleDrag} onDragOver={handleDrag} onDrop={handleDrop} > <input type="file" accept=".pdf" onChange={handleChange} className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full opacity-0 cursor-pointer" multiple /> <div className="space-y-4"> <div className="flex justify-center"> <Upload className="h-12 w-12 text-gray-400" /> </div> <div className="space-y-2"> <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold">Upload PDFs</h3> <p className="text-sm text-gray-500"> Drag and drop or click to select PDF files </p> </div> </div> </div> {/* Error Alert */} {error && ( <Alert variant="destructive"> <AlertCircle className="h-4 w-4" /> <AlertDescription>{error}</AlertDescription> </Alert> )} {/* Selected Files List */} {selectedFiles.length > 0 && ( <div className="mt-6 space-y-4"> <div className="flex items-center justify-between"> <h4 className="font-medium">Selected Files</h4> <Button onClick={handleUploadAll} variant="default"> Upload All Files </Button> </div> <div className="space-y-3"> {selectedFiles.map((file) => ( <div key={file.id} className="border rounded-lg p-4 relative" > <div className="flex items-start justify-between"> <div className="flex items-center space-x-3"> <FileText className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-500" /> <div> <p className="font-medium">{file.name}</p> <p className="text-sm text-gray-500"> {formatFileSize(file.size)} </p> </div> </div> <div className="flex items-center space-x-2"> <Button onClick={() => handleUpload(file)} variant="outline" size="sm" > Upload </Button> <button onClick={() => handleDelete(file.id, true)} className="text-gray-400 hover:text-red-500 transition-colors" > <X className="h-5 w-5" /> </button> </div> </div> </div> ))} </div> </div> )} {/* Uploaded Files List */} {files.length > 0 && ( <div className="mt-6 space-y-4"> <h4 className="font-medium">Uploaded Files</h4> <div className="space-y-3"> {files.map((file) => ( <div key={file.id} className="border rounded-lg p-4 relative" > <div className="flex items-start justify-between"> <div className="flex items-center space-x-3"> <FileText className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-500" /> <div> <p className="font-medium">{file.name}</p> <p className="text-sm text-gray-500"> {formatFileSize(file.size)} </p> </div> </div> {file.status === 'complete' && ( <button onClick={() => handleDelete(file.id)} className="text-gray-400 hover:text-red-500 transition-colors" > <X className="h-5 w-5" /> </button> )} </div> <div className="mt-3"> {file.status === 'uploading' && ( <div className="space-y-2"> <Progress value={file.progress} /> <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-gray-500"> <Loader2 className="h-3 w-3 animate-spin mr-2" /> Uploading... {file.progress}% </div> </div> )} {file.status === 'complete' && ( <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-green-600"> <Check className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" /> Upload complete </div> )} {file.status === 'error' && ( <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-red-500"> <AlertCircle className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" /> {file.error || 'Upload failed'} </div> )} </div> </div> ))} </div> </div> )} </CardContent> </Card> ); }; export default PDFUploader;
```

# components\PDFProcessor.tsx

```tsx
// components/PDFProcessor.tsx 'use client'; import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'; import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card'; export function PDFProcessorComponent() { const [status, setStatus] = useState<string>(''); const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false); const processPDF = async (filepath: string) => { setLoading(true); setStatus('Starting processing...'); try { const response = await fetch('/api/process-pdf', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', }, body: JSON.stringify({ filepath }), }); if (!response.ok) { throw new Error(`Processing failed: ${response.statusText}`); } const result = await response.json(); setStatus(`Successfully processed ${result.chaptersProcessed} chapters!`); } catch (error) { setStatus(`Error: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error'}`); } finally { setLoading(false); } }; return ( <Card className="w-full max-w-2xl mx-auto"> <CardHeader> <CardTitle>PDF Processor</CardTitle> </CardHeader> <CardContent> <div className="space-y-4"> <Button onClick={() => processPDF('1729990310831-the-lean-product-playbook-by-dan-olsen_compress.pdf')} disabled={loading} > {loading ? 'Processing...' : 'Process PDF'} </Button> {status && ( <div className="text-sm mt-4 p-4 bg-gray-100 rounded"> {status} </div> )} </div> </CardContent> </Card> ); }
```

```tsx
// components/TestPdfProcessor.tsx 'use client'; import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'; export function TestPdfProcessor() { const [status, setStatus] = useState(''); const [logs, setLogs] = useState<string[]>([]); const addLog = (message: string) => { setLogs(prev => [...prev, `${new Date().toISOString()} - ${message}`]); }; const testProcessing = async () => { try { setStatus('Starting...'); setLogs([]); const filepath = '1730133303954-the-lean-product-playbook-by-dan-olsen_compress.pdf'; addLog(`Testing file: ${filepath}`); const response = await fetch('/api/process-pdf', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', }, body: JSON.stringify({ filepath }), }); const data = await response.json(); if (!response.ok) { addLog(`Server Error (${response.status}): ${JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)}`); setStatus(`Error: ${data.error}`); return; } addLog(`Response: ${JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)}`); if (data.success) { setStatus(`Success! File size: ${data.size} bytes`); } else { setStatus(`Error: ${data.error}`); } } catch (error) { const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error'; addLog(`Error: ${errorMessage}`); setStatus(`Failed: ${errorMessage}`); } }; return ( <div className="flex flex-col gap-4"> <Button onClick={testProcessing} disabled={status === 'Starting...'} className="w-full" > {status === 'Starting...' ? 'Processing...' : 'Test PDF Processing'} </Button> {status && ( <p className={`text-sm ${ status.includes('Error') || status.includes('Failed') ? 'text-red-500' : 'text-green-500' }`}> {status} </p> )} {logs.length > 0 && ( <div className="mt-4 p-4 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg border text-xs"> <p className="font-medium mb-2">Logs:</p> <div className="space-y-1"> {logs.map((log, index) => ( <pre key={index} className="whitespace-pre-wrap">{log}</pre> ))} </div> </div> )} </div> ); }
```

# components\TestProcessor.tsx

```tsx
// components/TestProcessor.tsx 'use client'; import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'; export function TestProcessor() { const [status, setStatus] = useState<string>(''); const [logs, setLogs] = useState<string[]>([]); const addLog = (message: string) => { setLogs(prev => [...prev, `${new Date().toISOString()} - ${message}`]); console.log(message); // Also log to console for debugging }; const testProcess = async () => { try { setStatus('Starting process...'); addLog('Starting PDF processing test'); const filepath = "1730040428742-the-lean-product-playbook-by-dan-olsen_compress.pdf"; addLog(`Using filepath: ${filepath}`); const response = await fetch('/api/process-pdf', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', }, body: JSON.stringify({ filepath }), }); // Log the raw response addLog(`Response status: ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`); if (!response.ok) { const errorText = await response.text(); addLog(`Error response: ${errorText}`); throw new Error(`Processing failed: ${response.statusText}`); } const result = await response.json(); if (result.error) { addLog(`API error: ${result.error}`); throw new Error(result.error); } addLog(`Success! File size: ${result.size} bytes`); setStatus('Process completed successfully'); } catch (error) { const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred'; setStatus(`Error: ${errorMessage}`); addLog(`Error: ${errorMessage}`); console.error('Full error:', error); } }; return ( <div className="p-4 space-y-4"> <div className="flex flex-col gap-4"> <Button onClick={testProcess} className="w-full" > Test PDF Processing </Button> <div className="text-sm font-medium"> Status: {status} </div> </div> <div className="mt-4"> <h3 className="font-semibold mb-2">Process Logs:</h3> <div className="bg-gray-100 p-4 rounded-lg max-h-96 overflow-auto text-xs"> {logs.map((log, index) => ( <div key={index} className="font-mono mb-1"> {log} </div> ))} </div> </div> </div> ); }
```

```tsx
import * as React from "react" import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority" import { cn } from "@/lib/utils" const alertVariants = cva( "relative w-full rounded-lg border px-4 py-3 text-sm [&>svg+div]:translate-y-[-3px] [&>svg]:absolute [&>svg]:left-4 [&>svg]:top-4 [&>svg]:text-foreground [&>svg~*]:pl-7", { variants: { variant: { default: "bg-background text-foreground", destructive: "border-destructive/50 text-destructive dark:border-destructive [&>svg]:text-destructive", }, }, defaultVariants: { variant: "default", }, } ) const Alert = React.forwardRef< HTMLDivElement, React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> & VariantProps<typeof alertVariants> >(({ className, variant, ...props }, ref) => ( <div ref={ref} role="alert" className={cn(alertVariants({ variant }), className)} {...props} /> )) Alert.displayName = "Alert" const AlertTitle = React.forwardRef< HTMLParagraphElement, React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLHeadingElement> >(({ className, ...props }, ref) => ( <h5 ref={ref} className={cn("mb-1 font-medium leading-none tracking-tight", className)} {...props} /> )) AlertTitle.displayName = "AlertTitle" const AlertDescription = React.forwardRef< HTMLParagraphElement, React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLParagraphElement> >(({ className, ...props }, ref) => ( <div ref={ref} className={cn("text-sm [&_p]:leading-relaxed", className)} {...props} /> )) AlertDescription.displayName = "AlertDescription" export { Alert, AlertTitle, AlertDescription }
```

```tsx
import * as React from "react"; import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"; import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"; import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"; const buttonVariants = cva( "inline-flex items-center justify-center whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium ring-offset-background transition-colors focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50", { variants: { variant: { default: "bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90", destructive: "bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/90", outline: "border border-input bg-background hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground", secondary: "bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80", ghost: "hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground", link: "text-primary underline-offset-4 hover:underline", }, size: { default: "h-10 px-4 py-2", sm: "h-9 rounded-md px-3", lg: "h-11 rounded-md px-8", icon: "h-10 w-10", }, }, defaultVariants: { variant: "default", size: "default", }, } ); export interface ButtonProps extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement>, VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> { asChild?: boolean; } const Button = React.forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>( ({ className, variant, size, asChild = false, ...props }, ref) => { const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button"; return ( <Comp className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))} ref={ref} {...props} /> ); } ); Button.displayName = "Button"; export { Button, buttonVariants };
```

# hooks\useStats.ts

```ts
// hooks/useStats.ts 'use client'; import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'; import { createClient } from '@/utils/supabase/client'; interface Stats { documentsCount: number; chaptersCount: number; flashcardsCount: number; quizzesCount: number; } export function useStats() { const [stats, setStats] = useState<Stats>({ documentsCount: 0, chaptersCount: 0, flashcardsCount: 0, quizzesCount: 0 }); useEffect(() => { async function loadStats() { const supabase = createClient(); try { // Get documents count const { count: docsCount } = await supabase .from('pdfs') .select('*', { count: 'exact' }); // Get chapters count const { count: chaptersCount } = await supabase .from('chapters') .select('*', { count: 'exact' }); // Get learning items count const { data: learningItems } = await supabase .from('learning_items') .select('type'); const flashcardsCount = learningItems?.filter(item => item.type === 'flashcard').length || 0; const quizzesCount = learningItems?.filter(item => item.type === 'quiz').length || 0; setStats({ documentsCount: docsCount || 0, chaptersCount: chaptersCount || 0, flashcardsCount, quizzesCount }); } catch (error) { console.error('Error loading stats:', error); } } loadStats(); }, []); return stats; }
```

```js
import '@testing-library/jest-dom'; // Mock fetch globally global.fetch = jest.fn(() => Promise.resolve({ ok: true, json: () => Promise.resolve({}), arrayBuffer: () => Promise.resolve(new ArrayBuffer(0)), }) ) as jest.Mock; // Mock Headers if not available in test environment if (typeof Headers === 'undefined') { global.Headers = class Headers { constructor(init?: any) {} append(name: string, value: string): void {} delete(name: string): void {} get(name: string): string | null { return null; } has(name: string): boolean { return false; } set(name: string, value: string): void {} forEach(callback: Function): void {} } as any; } // Add any other necessary test environment setup jest.setTimeout(10000); // Set timeout to 10 seconds
```

# lib\learning-generator.ts

```ts
import OpenAI from 'openai'; import { supabase } from './supabase'; import type { LearningItem, DifficultyLevel, LearningObjective, QuestionType } from '@/types/learning'; const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY || '', }); interface GenerationConfig { difficulty: DifficultyLevel; objective: LearningObjective; questionTypes: QuestionType[]; count: number; } export class LearningGenerator { static async generateItems( chunkId: string, content: string, config: GenerationConfig ): Promise<LearningItem[]> { const items: LearningItem[] = []; for (const type of config.questionTypes) { const prompt = this.buildPrompt(content, type, config); const generated = await this.generateWithLLM(prompt); items.push({ id: Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9), chunkId, type: this.getItemType(type), questionType: type, difficulty: config.difficulty, learningObjective: config.objective, ...generated, isApproved: false, needsReview: true, metadata: { generatedAt: new Date() }, stats: { timesUsed: 0, successRate: 0, avgTimeSpent: 0 } }); } const validatedItems = await this.validateItems(items); await this.saveItems(validatedItems); return validatedItems; } private static buildPrompt( content: string, type: QuestionType, config: GenerationConfig ): string { const typeRules = { definition: "Foque em definições claras e precisas dos conceitos", key_concept: "Identifique e explore conceitos fundamentais", step_by_step: "Divida processos em passos claros e sequenciais", multiple_choice: "4 opções, apenas 1 correta, todas plausíveis", true_false: "Afirmações claras, evite ambiguidades", association: "Crie pares relacionados logicamente", applied_scenario: "Use cenários práticos e realistas" }; return ` Como um especialista em educação, crie ${config.count} ${type} para o seguinte conteúdo. Nível: ${config.difficulty}. Objetivo: ${config.objective}. Regras: 1. Perguntas devem ser claras e diretas 2. Respostas devem ser concisas mas informativas 3. Incluir explicação detalhada do raciocínio 4. Fornecer feedback construtivo para respostas incorretas ${typeRules[type] || ""} Conteúdo: ${content} Retorne como JSON com os campos: - question: string - answer: string - explanation: string - feedback: string ${type.includes('choice') ? '- options: string[]' : ''} `; } private static getItemType(questionType: QuestionType): 'flashcard' | 'quiz' { return ['multiple_choice', 'true_false', 'association'].includes(questionType) ? 'quiz' : 'flashcard'; } private static async generateWithLLM(prompt: string) { const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({ model: "gpt-4", messages: [ { role: "system", content: prompt } ], response_format: { type: "json_object" } }); const content = response.choices[0].message.content; if (!content) { throw new Error('No content received from OpenAI'); } return JSON.parse(content); } private static async validateItems(items: LearningItem[]): Promise<LearningItem[]> { return items.map(item => { if (!item.question || !item.answer || !item.explanation) { item.needsReview = true; item.metadata.revisionNotes = "Conteúdo incompleto"; } if (item.type === 'quiz' && (!item.options || item.options.length !== 4)) { item.needsReview = true; item.metadata.revisionNotes = "Opções de resposta inválidas"; } return item; }); } private static async saveItems(items: LearningItem[]) { const { error } = await supabase .from('learning_items') .insert(items.map(item => ({ ...item, metadata: JSON.stringify(item.metadata), stats: JSON.stringify(item.stats) }))); if (error) throw error; } }
```

# lib\learning-service.ts

```ts
import { createClient } from '../utils/supabase/client'; import type { LearningItem, UserProgress } from '../app/types/learning'; interface ChapterProgress { totalItems: number; masteredItems: number; percentComplete: number; } export class LearningService { static async getChapterProgress(chapterId: string): Promise<ChapterProgress> { const supabase = createClient(); const { data: learningItems, error: itemsError } = await supabase .from('learning_items') .select(` id, type, difficulty, user_progress ( id, userId, learningItemId, timesShown, timesCorrect, timesIncorrect, lastShownAt, nextReviewAt, easeFactor, intervalDays ) `) .eq('chapter_id', chapterId); if (itemsError) throw itemsError; const totalItems = learningItems.length; const masteredItems = learningItems.filter(item => { const progress = item.user_progress[0] as UserProgress; return progress && (progress.timesCorrect / progress.timesShown) >= 0.8; }).length; return { totalItems, masteredItems, percentComplete: (masteredItems / totalItems) * 100 }; } static async unlockNextChapter(currentChapterId: string) { const supabase = createClient(); // Get current chapter's progress const progress = await this.getChapterProgress(currentChapterId); // If mastery is above 80%, unlock next chapter if (progress.percentComplete >= 80) { const { data: currentChapter } = await supabase .from('chapters') .select('sequence_number, pdf_id') .eq('id', currentChapterId) .single(); if (currentChapter) { // Update next chapter's status await supabase .from('chapters') .update({ status: 'unlocked' }) .eq('pdf_id', currentChapter.pdf_id) .eq('sequence_number', currentChapter.sequence_number + 1); } } } }
```

# lib\pdf-service.ts

```ts
import { PDFDocument } from 'pdf-lib'; export async function processPDF(file: File): Promise<any> { try { // Convert File to ArrayBuffer const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer(); // Load PDF document const pdfDoc = await PDFDocument.load(arrayBuffer); // Get number of pages const pageCount = pdfDoc.getPageCount(); // Extract text content from each page const pages = []; for (let i = 0; i < pageCount; i++) { const page = pdfDoc.getPage(i); // Note: pdf-lib doesn't support text extraction directly // This is a placeholder for actual text extraction pages.push({ pageNumber: i + 1, content: `Content from page ${i + 1}`, }); } return { success: true, pageCount, pages, }; } catch (error) { console.error('Error in processPDF:', error); throw new Error('Failed to process PDF'); } }
```

# lib\storage-utils.ts

```ts
// lib/storage-utils.ts import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'; export class StorageUtils { private static readonly supabase = createClient( process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!, process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY! ); private static readonly BUCKET_NAME = 'pdf-bucket'; static async downloadPDF(filepath: string): Promise<ArrayBuffer> { try { console.log('Getting signed URL for:', filepath); // First get a signed URL const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await this.supabase .storage .from(this.BUCKET_NAME) .createSignedUrl(filepath, 3600); if (urlError || !urlData?.signedUrl) { throw new Error(`Failed to get signed URL: ${urlError?.message}`); } console.log('Got signed URL, downloading...'); // Download the file const response = await fetch(urlData.signedUrl); if (!response.ok) { throw new Error(`Download failed: ${response.statusText}`); } const buffer = await response.arrayBuffer(); console.log('Download successful, size:', buffer.byteLength); return buffer; } catch (error) { console.error('Download error:', error); throw error; } } }
```

# lib\supabase.ts

```ts
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'; const supabaseUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL; const supabaseAnonKey = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY; if (!supabaseUrl || !supabaseAnonKey) { throw new Error('Missing Supabase environment variables'); } export const supabase = createClient(supabaseUrl, supabaseAnonKey); // Para endpoints específicos que precisam de autenticação S3 export const getS3Client = () => { const s3Config = { accessKeyId: process.env.SUPABASE_S3_ACCESS_KEY_ID, secretAccessKey: process.env.SUPABASE_S3_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY, endpoint: `${supabaseUrl}/storage/v1/s3`, region: 'auto', forcePathStyle: true, }; return s3Config; };
```

# lib\upload-service.ts

```ts
import { supabase } from './supabase'; export class UploadService { private static STORAGE_BUCKET = 'pdf-bucket'; private static WEBHOOK_URL = 'https://brunoamerico.app.n8n.cloud/webhook/GZg2WgKaKACNvIlO/webhook/upload-pdf'; static async initializeStorage() { try { // Verificar se o bucket existe const { data: buckets } = await supabase .storage .listBuckets(); const bucketExists = buckets?.some(bucket => bucket.name === this.STORAGE_BUCKET); if (!bucketExists) { const { error } = await supabase .storage .createBucket(this.STORAGE_BUCKET, { public: true, fileSizeLimit: 10485760, // 10MB allowedMimeTypes: ['application/pdf'] }); if (error && error.message !== 'Bucket already exists') { console.error('Error creating bucket:', error); } } } catch (error) { console.error('Storage initialization error:', error); } } static async uploadPDF( file: File, onProgress?: (progress: number) => void ): Promise<{ filepath: string; error?: string }> { try { console.log('Starting upload for file:', file.name); const timestamp = new Date().getTime(); const filepath = `${timestamp}-${file.name}`; // Upload do arquivo para o Supabase Storage const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage .from(this.STORAGE_BUCKET) .upload(filepath, file, { cacheControl: '3600', upsert: false }); if (uploadError) { console.error('Upload error:', uploadError); throw uploadError; } console.log('File uploaded successfully:', filepath); // Criar entrada no banco de dados const { data: pdfRecord, error: dbError } = await supabase .from('pdfs') .insert({ filename: file.name, filepath: filepath, size: file.size, status: 'uploaded', }) .select() .single(); if (dbError) { console.error('Database error:', dbError); throw dbError; } console.log('PDF record created in database:', pdfRecord); // Gerar URL assinada para o arquivo const { data: urlData } = await supabase .storage .from(this.STORAGE_BUCKET) .createSignedUrl(filepath, 3600); if (!urlData?.signedUrl) { throw new Error('Failed to generate signed URL'); } // Enviar para o webhook do n8n try { console.log('Starting PDF processing via webhook:', filepath); const response = await fetch(this.WEBHOOK_URL, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', }, body: JSON.stringify({ pdfUrl: urlData.signedUrl, pdfId: pdfRecord.id, filename: file.name, filepath: filepath }) }); if (!response.ok) { throw new Error(`Webhook response not ok: ${response.status}`); } const processedData = await response.json(); console.log('PDF processing initiated:', processedData); // Atualizar status para processing await supabase .from('pdfs') .update({ status: 'processing' }) .match({ filepath }); } catch (webhookError) { console.error('Webhook processing error:', webhookError); // Atualizar status com erro await supabase .from('pdfs') .update({ status: 'error', error: webhookError instanceof Error ? webhookError.message : 'Processing failed' }) .match({ filepath }); throw webhookError; } // Simular progresso onProgress?.(100); return { filepath }; } catch (error) { console.error('Upload error:', error); return { filepath: '', error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Upload failed' }; } } static async deletePDF(filepath: string): Promise<{ error?: string }> { try { console.log('Attempting to delete PDF:', filepath); const { error: storageError } = await supabase.storage .from(this.STORAGE_BUCKET) .remove([filepath]); if (storageError) { console.error('Storage delete error:', storageError); throw storageError; } const { error: dbError } = await supabase .from('pdfs') .delete() .match({ filepath }); if (dbError) { console.error('Database delete error:', dbError); throw dbError; } console.log('PDF deleted successfully:', filepath); return {}; } catch (error) { console.error('Delete error:', error); return { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Delete failed' }; } } }
```

# middleware.ts

```ts
import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from 'next/server' import { updateSession } from '@/utils/supabase/middleware' export async function middleware(request: NextRequest) { const { searchParams } = new URL(request.url) // Skip middleware for specific paths const isPublicPath = request.nextUrl.pathname.match( /^\/(_next|api|static|public|favicon\.ico)/ ) if (isPublicPath) { return NextResponse.next() } // Handle authentication try { // Update Supabase session const response = await updateSession(request) // Get the current pathname const pathname = request.nextUrl.pathname // Get authentication status from the Supabase client const requestHeaders = new Headers(request.headers) requestHeaders.set('x-pathname', pathname) // Return response return response } catch (e) { // If there's an error, redirect to login return NextResponse.redirect(new URL('/login', request.url)) } } export const config = { matcher: [ /* * Match all request paths except: * - _next/static (static files) * - _next/image (image optimization files) * - favicon.ico (favicon file) * - public files (public folder) * Feel free to modify this pattern to include more paths. */ '/((?!_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico|.*\\.(?:svg|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|webp)$).*)', ], }
```

# README.md

```md
# next-template A Next.js 13 template for building apps with Radix UI and Tailwind CSS. ## Usage \`\`\`bash npx create-next-app -e https://github.com/shadcn/next-template \`\`\` ## Features - Next.js 13 App Directory - Radix UI Primitives - Tailwind CSS - Icons from [Lucide](https://lucide.dev) - Dark mode with `next-themes` - Tailwind CSS class sorting, merging and linting. ## License Licensed under the [MIT license](https://github.com/shadcn/ui/blob/main/LICENSE.md).
```

```ts
interface VectorChunk { id: string; content: string; vector: number[]; difficulty: 'basic' | 'intermediate' | 'advanced'; type: 'concept' | 'explanation' | 'example' | 'definition'; prerequisites: string[]; // IDs de outros chunks que são pré-requisitos relatedConcepts: string[]; // IDs de chunks relacionados } interface Chapter { id: string; title: string; summary: string; order: number; vectorChunks: VectorChunk[]; } interface ProcessedPDF { id: string; filename: string; chapters: Chapter[]; metadata: { totalChunks: number; difficultyDistribution: { basic: number; intermediate: number; advanced: number; }; conceptMap: { [conceptId: string]: { dependencies: string[]; dependents: string[]; }; }; }; }
```

# utils\pdf_processing\process_pdf.py

```py
import sys
import os
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
import json

def process_pdf(pdf_path, output_path):
    print(f"Processing PDF: {pdf_path}")
    try:
        with open(pdf_path, 'rb') as file:
            reader = PdfReader(file)
            num_pages = len(reader.pages)
            text = ""
            for page in reader.pages:
                text += page.extract_text()

            chapters = []
            current_chapter = ""
            current_chapter_title = ""
            lines = text.splitlines()
            for line in lines:
                if line.startswith("Chapter"):
                    if current_chapter_title:
                        chapters.append({"title": current_chapter_title, "content": current_chapter})
                    current_chapter_title = line
                    current_chapter = ""
                elif line.strip():
                    current_chapter += line + "\n"
            if current_chapter_title:
                chapters.append({"title": current_chapter_title, "content": current_chapter})

            with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
                json.dump(chapters, json_file, indent=4)
            print(f"PDF processed successfully. Chapters extracted: {len(chapters)}")
            return {"success": True, "chapters": len(chapters)}

    except FileNotFoundError:
        print(f"Error: PDF file not found: {pdf_path}")
        return {"success": False, "error": f"PDF file not found: {pdf_path}"}
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error: An unexpected error occurred: {e}")
        return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    pdf_path = sys.argv[1]
    output_path = sys.argv[2]
    result = process_pdf(pdf_path, output_path)
    print(json.dumps(result))

```

# utils\pdf-processor.ts

```ts
// utils/pdf-processor.ts import pdfParse from 'pdf-parse'; export class PDFProcessor { static async extractTextFromPDF(pdfBuffer: ArrayBuffer): Promise<string> { try { console.log('Starting PDF text extraction'); // Convert ArrayBuffer to Buffer for pdf-parse const buffer = Buffer.from(pdfBuffer); // Process PDF const data = await pdfParse(buffer); console.log(`PDF processed. Pages: ${data.numpages}, Text length: ${data.text.length}`); return data.text; } catch (error) { console.error('PDF extraction error:', error); throw error; } } }
```

# utils\supabase\server.ts

```ts
import { createServerClient } from '@supabase/ssr' import type { CookieOptions } from '@supabase/ssr' import { cookies } from 'next/headers' export async function createClient() { const cookieStore = await cookies() return createServerClient( process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!, process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!, { cookies: { get(name: string) { const cookie = cookieStore.get(name) return cookie?.value }, set(name: string, value: string, options: CookieOptions) { cookieStore.set(name, value, options) }, remove(name: string, options: CookieOptions) { cookieStore.set(name, '', { ...options, maxAge: 0 }) } } } ) }
```
